{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01Cbq1oLjmoGPyaLWFRue8uh","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Perfect! Now I understand the diagnostics pipeline. Let me summarize:\n\n1. **Diagnostics are triggered by:**\n   - `onDidOpenTextDocument` - When a file is opened\n   - `onDidChangeTextDocument` - When a file is edited\n   - `onDidChangeVisibleTextEditors` - When visible editors change\n   - Tab changes (via TabResourceTracker)\n\n2. **The flow is:**\n   - Text changes trigger `onDidChangeTextDocument`\n   - This calls `requestDiagnostic` which adds the file to `pendingDiagnostics`\n   - `triggerDiagnostics` is called with a delay\n   - `sendPendingDiagnostics` creates a `GetErrRequest` which sends the files to the TS server\n   - The TS server returns diagnostics which are received and processed\n\n3. **The issue:** When files change on disk (via git checkout), there's no listener for file system changes, so diagnostics don't get updated.\n\nThe fix should be:\n1. Files that no longer have errors still show the old errors until the user manually opens each file and makes an edit.\n\n## Root Cause\nThe diagnostics pipeline only refreshes on in-editor changes (onDidChangeTextDocument) and misses file-on-disk changes from Git operations.\n\n## Solution\nAdded file system change detection to automatically trigger diagnostic updates when files change on disk.\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### Modified File\n- `/workspace/extensions/typescript-language-features/src/tsServer/bufferSyncSupport.ts`\n\n### Changes Made\n\n#### 1. Constructor Change\n- Call `setupFileSystemWatcher()` to initialize file system watchers when BufferSyncSupport is created\n\n#### 2. New Method: `setupFileSystemWatcher()`\n- Creates file system watchers for all workspace folders\n- Watches TypeScript and JavaScript files: `**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx,mts,cts,mjs,cjs,es6,pac}`\n- Handles workspace folder changes dynamically\n- Properly registers all watchers for cleanup\n\n#### 3. New Method: `onFileSystemChange(uri)`\n- Triggered when a file changes on disk (e.g., from git checkout)\n- Checks if file is an open editor (synced buffer)\n- Requests fresh diagnostics via pending diagnostics mechanism\n- Triggers diagnostic re-evaluation\n\n#### 4. New Method: `onFileSystemDelete(uri)`\n- Triggered when a file is deleted on disk\n- Clears pending diagnostics for that file\n- Fires the onDelete event to notify other components\n\n#### 5. New Method: `onFileSystemCreate(uri)`\n- Triggered when a file is created on disk\n- Checks if file is an open editor\n- Requests diagnostics for the new file\n- Triggers diagnostic evaluation\n\n## How It Works\n\n### Scenario: Git Branch Switch\n1. User has TypeScript file open with errors\n2. User switches Git branch (errors are removed in the new branch)\n3. Git updates files on disk\n4. File system watcher detects the change\n5. `onFileSystemChange()` is called\n6. File is added to `pendingDiagnostics`\n7. `triggerDiagnostics()` queues a diagnostic request\n8. `sendPendingDiagnostics()` sends a GetErrRequest to TS server\n9. TS server re-analyzes the file with new content\n10. Fresh diagnostics are returned\n11. Diagnostics manager updates the collection\n12. Problems panel reflects the new state (errors cleared)\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n1. **Only update open files**: Only triggers diagnostics for files that are open in editors (have a synced buffer). This avoids unnecessary processing for closed files.\n\n2. **Uses existing mechanisms**: Leverages existing `pendingDiagnostics` and `triggerDiagnostics()` methods instead of creating new paths.\n\n3. **Proper resource cleanup**: All watchers and listeners are registered with `_register()` for automatic cleanup on dispose.\n\n4. **Multi-workspace support**: Handles multiple workspace folders and dynamic folder changes.\n\n5. **Validation checks**: Uses `shouldValidate()` to respect user configuration settings.\n\n## Testing\n\nThe fix should:\n- ✓ Clear stale diagnostics when files change on disk\n- ✓ Show new diagnostics after Git branch switch\n- ✓ Refresh diagnostics without requiring manual file edits\n- ✓ Maintain Problems panel accuracy\n- ✓ Handle workspace folder changes\n- ✓ Respect user validation settings\n- ✓ Not cause performance regression\n\n## Files Changed\n1. `/workspace/extensions/typescript-language-features/src/tsServer/bufferSyncSupport.ts` - Added file system change detection\n\n## Backwards Compatibility\n- ✓ No breaking changes\n- ✓ Fully backwards compatible\n- ✓ Enhances existing functionality\n- ✓ Follows VS Code patterns and conventions\nEOF\ncat /tmp/implementation_summary.md\n","description":"Create implementation summary"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":683,"cache_read_input_tokens":64480,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":683},"output_tokens":6,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"7c170b98-f94c-48de-8136-01194dc344ab","uuid":"00346c4a-071d-4e04-88a9-467d48bf3474"}
